DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `delivery_configs`;
CREATE TABLE `delivery_configs` (
  `id` int(11) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `type` varchar(50) NOT NULL DEFAULT 'now',
  `time_take` int(11) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `time_slots` text CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci,
  `status` tinyint(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT '1',
  `created_at` datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  `updated_at` datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `delivery_counts`;

  `id` bigint(20) unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,

  `status` tinyint(4) NOT NULL DEFAULT '1',
  `created_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `updated_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_unicode_ci;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `failed_jobs`;
CREATE TABLE `failed_jobs` (
  `id` bigint(20) unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `uuid` varchar(191) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL,
  `connection` text COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL,
  `queue` text COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL,
  `payload` longtext COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL,
  `exception` longtext COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL,
  `failed_at` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  UNIQUE KEY `failed_jobs_uuid_unique` (`uuid`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_unicode_ci;


DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `feedback`;
CREATE TABLE `feedback` (
  `id` bigint(20) unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `user_id` bigint(20) unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `subject` varchar(191) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `experience` varchar(191) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `message` text COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci,
  `status` tinyint(4) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `created_at` datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  `updated_at` datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `feedback_user_id_foreign` (`user_id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_unicode_ci;


DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `floating_cashes`;
CREATE TABLE `floating_cashes` (
  `id` bigint(20) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `order_id` bigint(20) unsigned NOT NULL,
  `amount` float(16,2) NOT NULL,
  `user_id` bigint(20) unsigned NOT NULL,
  `delivery_boy_id` bigint(20) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `status` tinyint(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT '1' COMMENT '1->cash_pick, 2->handover',
  `created_at` datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  `updated_at` datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `order_id` (`order_id`),
  KEY `user_id` (`user_id`),
  CONSTRAINT `floating_cashes_ibfk_3` FOREIGN KEY (`order_id`) REFERENCES `orders` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE ON UPDATE CASCADE,
  CONSTRAINT `floating_cashes_ibfk_4` FOREIGN KEY (`user_id`) REFERENCES `users` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE ON UPDATE CASCADE
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1;


DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `frequencies`;
CREATE TABLE `frequencies` (
  `id` bigint(20) unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `name` varchar(191) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `days` int(11) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `description` text COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci,
  `skip_days` int(11) DEFAULT NULL,
  `position` int(11) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `status` tinyint(4) NOT NULL DEFAULT '1' COMMENT '0->inactive,1->active,2->deleted',
  `created_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `updated_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_unicode_ci;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `jobs`;
CREATE TABLE `jobs` (
  `id` bigint(20) unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `queue` varchar(191) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL,
  `payload` longtext COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL,
  `attempts` tinyint(3) unsigned NOT NULL,
  `reserved_at` int(10) unsigned DEFAULT NULL,
  `available_at` int(10) unsigned NOT NULL,
  `created_at` int(10) unsigned NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `jobs_queue_index` (`queue`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_unicode_ci;


DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `locations`;
CREATE TABLE `locations` (
  `id` bigint(20) unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `name` varchar(191) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `location` text COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci,
  `pincode` varchar(191) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `lat` varchar(191) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `lon` varchar(191) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `status` tinyint(4) NOT NULL DEFAULT '1',
  `position` int(11) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `created_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `updated_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_unicode_ci;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `notifications`;
CREATE TABLE `notifications` (
  `id` bigint(20) unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `type` tinyint(4) NOT NULL DEFAULT '1' COMMENT '1->single,2->all',
  `user_id` bigint(20) unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `title` varchar(191) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `body` text COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci,
  `image` varchar(191) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `payload` text COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci,
  `status` tinyint(4) NOT NULL DEFAULT '1',
  `show_in_app` tinyint(4) NOT NULL DEFAULT '1',
  `seen` tinyint(4) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `user_type` tinyint(4) NOT NULL DEFAULT '2' COMMENT '2->users,3->delivery boy,4->city admin',
  `created_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `updated_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_unicode_ci;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `oauth_access_tokens`;
CREATE TABLE `oauth_access_tokens` (
  `id` varchar(100) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL,
  `user_id` bigint(20) unsigned DEFAULT NULL,
  `client_id` bigint(20) unsigned NOT NULL,
  `name` varchar(191) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `scopes` text COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci,
  `revoked` tinyint(1) NOT NULL,
  `created_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `updated_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `expires_at` datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `oauth_access_tokens_user_id_index` (`user_id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_unicode_ci;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `oauth_auth_codes`;
CREATE TABLE `oauth_auth_codes` (
  `id` varchar(100) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL,
  `user_id` bigint(20) unsigned NOT NULL,
  `client_id` bigint(20) unsigned NOT NULL,
  `scopes` text COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci,
  `revoked` tinyint(1) NOT NULL,
  `expires_at` datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `oauth_auth_codes_user_id_index` (`user_id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_unicode_ci;


DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `oauth_clients`;
CREATE TABLE `oauth_clients` (
  `id` bigint(20) unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `user_id` bigint(20) unsigned DEFAULT NULL,
  `name` varchar(191) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL,
  `secret` varchar(100) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `provider` varchar(191) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `redirect` text COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL,
  `personal_access_client` tinyint(1) NOT NULL,
  `password_client` tinyint(1) NOT NULL,
  `revoked` tinyint(1) NOT NULL,
  `created_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `updated_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `oauth_clients_user_id_index` (`user_id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_unicode_ci;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `oauth_personal_access_clients`;
CREATE TABLE `oauth_personal_access_clients` (
  `id` bigint(20) unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `client_id` bigint(20) unsigned NOT NULL,
  `created_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `updated_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`)

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `oauth_refresh_tokens`;
CREATE TABLE `oauth_refresh_tokens` (
  `id` varchar(100) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL,
  `access_token_id` varchar(100) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL,
  `revoked` tinyint(1) NOT NULL,
  `expires_at` datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `oauth_refresh_tokens_access_token_id_index` (`access_token_id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_unicode_ci;


DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `orders`;
CREATE TABLE `orders` (
  `id` bigint(20) unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `user_id` bigint(20) unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `subtotal` double(16,2) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0.00',
  `discount` double(16,2) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0.00' COMMENT 'this is total discount addition of coupon and other discounts',
  `coupon_discount` double(16,2) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0.00',
  `cashback_discount` double(16,2) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0.00',
  `gst` double(16,2) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0.00',
  `delivery_charges` double(16,2) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0.00',
  `payable_amount` double(16,2) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0.00',
  `coupon_id` int(11) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `shipping_name` varchar(191) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `shipping_address_type` varchar(20) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `shipping_phone` varchar(191) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `shipping_flat` varchar(191) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `shipping_pincode` varchar(191) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `shipping_area` varchar(191) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `shipping_landmark` varchar(191) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `shipping_location` text COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci,
  `payment_mode` varchar(191) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT 'online' COMMENT 'cod,online',
  `delivery_boy_id` bigint(20) unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `warehouse_id` bigint(20) unsigned NOT NULL,
  `status` tinyint(4) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '0->pending,1->confirmed,2->delivered,3->cancel by user,4->cancel_by_admin',
  `is_paid` tinyint(4) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '0->not_paid,1->paid',
  `txn_id` varchar(200) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `cancel_at` datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  `created_at` datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  `updated_at` datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  `lat` varchar(191) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `lng` varchar(191) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `warehouse_lat` varchar(191) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `warehouse_lng` varchar(191) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `warehouse_address` varchar(255) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `warehouse_name` varchar(255) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `cancel_reason` text COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci,
  `deliver_boy_subscription_id` int(11) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `delivery_date` datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  `is_any_product_return` tinyint(4) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `assign_time` datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  `pickup_time` datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  `is_pickup` tinyint(1) DEFAULT '0',
  `reach_time` datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  `completed_at` datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  `is_refunded` int(11) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `paid_amount` double(16,2) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0.00',
  `confirmation_otp` varchar(100) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `payable_deliveries_count` int(11) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `order_type` tinyint(4) NOT NULL DEFAULT '1' COMMENT '1->buyOnce,2->subscribe',
  `delivery_type` varchar(20) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT 'now',
  `schedule_date` date DEFAULT NULL,
  `schedule_time` varchar(50) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `is_any_product_cancel` tinyint(4) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `cancel_by` varchar(20) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT 'customer' COMMENT 'customer | deliveryboy',
  `step` int(11) NOT NULL DEFAULT '1',
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_unicode_ci;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `order_histories`;
CREATE TABLE `order_histories` (
  `id` bigint(20) unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `order_id` bigint(20) unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `user_id` bigint(20) unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `product_id` bigint(20) unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `product_name` varchar(100) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `product_image` varchar(100) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `product_mrp` float(16,2) DEFAULT NULL,
  `product_discount` float(16,2) DEFAULT NULL,
  `qty` int(11) NOT NULL DEFAULT '1',
  `unit_price` float(16,2) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0.00',
  `order_type` tinyint(4) NOT NULL DEFAULT '1' COMMENT '1->buyOnce,2->subscribe',
  `price` double(16,2) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0.00' COMMENT 'total',
  `deliveries` int(11) NOT NULL DEFAULT '1' COMMENT 'this will eligible in case of order_type -> 2',
  `deliveries_done` int(11) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `start_date` datetime DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'this will eligible in case of order_type -> 2',
  `shipping_name` varchar(191) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `shipping_phone` varchar(191) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `shipping_flat` varchar(191) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `shipping_pincode` varchar(191) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `shipping_location` text COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci,
  `status` tinyint(4) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '0->pending, 1->accepted or start, 2->completed, 3->cancelled,4->stopped',
  `created_at` datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  `updated_at` datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  `skip_days` int(11) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `vacations` text COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci,
  `end_date` datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  `skip_dates` longtext COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci,
  `non_skip_dates` longtext COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci,
  `delivery_date` datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  `actual_qty` int(11) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT 'product actual quantity of one piece',
  `unit` varchar(191) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `order_id` (`order_id`),
  CONSTRAINT `order_histories_ibfk_2` FOREIGN KEY (`order_id`) REFERENCES `orders` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE ON UPDATE CASCADE
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_unicode_ci;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `otp_users`;
CREATE TABLE `otp_users` (
  `id` bigint(20) unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `name` varchar(191) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `email` varchar(191) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `password` varchar(255) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `referral_from` varchar(255) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `phone` varchar(191) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `email_verified` tinyint(4) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `phone_verified` tinyint(4) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `otp` varchar(191) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `otp_email` varchar(191) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `is_verified` tinyint(1) DEFAULT '0',
  `user_type` tinyint(4) NOT NULL DEFAULT '2' COMMENT '1->admin,2->users,3->delivery_boy',
  `created_at` datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  `updated_at` datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_unicode_ci;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `partners`;
CREATE TABLE `partners` (
  `id` int(11) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `image` varchar(100) NOT NULL DEFAULT 'default.png',
  `position` int(11) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `type` int(11) NOT NULL DEFAULT '1' COMMENT '1->press release, 2->partners',
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1;

INSERT INTO `partners` (`id`, `image`, `position`, `type`) VALUES
(1,	'default.png',	1,	1),
(2,	'default1.png',	1,	2);

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `password_resets`;
CREATE TABLE `password_resets` (
  `email` varchar(191) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL,
  `token` varchar(191) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL,
  `created_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  KEY `password_resets_email_index` (`email`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_unicode_ci;


DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `plans`;
CREATE TABLE `plans` (
  `id` bigint(20) unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `name` varchar(191) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `amount` double(16,2) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0.00',
  `benefit` double(16,2) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0.00',
  `position` int(11) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `status` tinyint(4) NOT NULL DEFAULT '1',
  `created_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `updated_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_unicode_ci;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `products`;
CREATE TABLE `products` (
  `id` bigint(20) unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `code` varchar(255) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `category_id` bigint(20) unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `subcategory_id` bigint(20) unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `name` varchar(191) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `image` varchar(191) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT 'default.png',
  `attributes` longtext COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci,
  `mrp` double(16,2) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0.00',
  `discount` double(16,2) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0.00',
  `discount_type` tinyint(4) NOT NULL DEFAULT '1' COMMENT '1->%,2->flat',
  `selling_price` double(16,2) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0.00',
  `subscription_price` double(16,2) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0.00',
  `show_in_subscriptions` tinyint(4) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '0->no,1->yes',
  `stock` int(11) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `qty` int(11) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `no_of_pieces` varchar(100) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `serves` varchar(100) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `cooking_time` varchar(100) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `net_wt` varchar(100) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `gross_wt` varchar(100) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `tags` varchar(100) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `unit` varchar(191) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `position` int(11) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `hifen_name` varchar(255) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `status` tinyint(4) NOT NULL DEFAULT '1' COMMENT '0->inactive,1->active,2->deleted',
  `mark_as_new` tinyint(4) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '0->no,1->yes',
  `created_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `updated_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `added_by` bigint(20) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `description` text COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci,
  `mark_as_bestoffers` tinyint(4) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `mark_as_hotselling` tinyint(4) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `category_ids_string` varchar(255) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `is_combo` tinyint(4) DEFAULT '0',
  `packing_type` varchar(100) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `gallery` text COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci,
  `rating` varchar(300) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL COMMENT '{"average":0,"total_reviews":0}',
  `hover_image` varchar(100) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT 'default1.png',
  `is_deal` tinyint(1) DEFAULT '0',
  `start_date` datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  `end_date` datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_unicode_ci;

A male that has been&nbsp;<a href=\"https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Castrated\">castrated</a>&nbsp;is a&nbsp;<strong><a href=\"https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Capon\">capon</a></strong>. An adult female bird is called a&nbsp;<strong>hen</strong>&nbsp;and a sexually immature female is called a&nbsp;<strong>pullet</strong>.</p>\r\n\r\n<p>Originally raised for&nbsp;<a href=\"https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Cockfight\">cockfighting</a>&nbsp;or for special ceremonies, chickens were not kept for food until the&nbsp;<a href=\"https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hellenistic_period\">Hellenistic period</a>&nbsp;(4th&ndash;2nd centuries BC).<a href=\"https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Chicken#cite_note-npr.org-1\">[1]</a><a href=\"https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Chicken#cite_note-pmid26195775-2\">[2]</a>&nbsp;Humans now keep chickens primarily as a source of food (consuming both their&nbsp;<a href=\"https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Chicken_as_food\">meat</a>&nbsp;and&nbsp;<a href=\"https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Egg_as_food\">eggs</a>) and as&nbsp;<a href=\"https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Pet\">pets</a>.</p>\r\n\r\n<p>Chickens are one of the most common and widespread&nbsp;<a href=\"https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Domestic_animals\">domestic animals</a>, with a total population of 23.7 billion as of 2018,<a href=\"https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Chicken#cite_note-3\">[3]</a>&nbsp;up from more than 19 billion in 2011.<a href=\"https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Chicken#cite_note-2011-19-billion-chickens-4\">[4]</a>&nbsp;There are more chickens in the world than any other&nbsp;<a href=\"https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bird\">bird</a>.<a href=\"https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Chicken#cite_note-2011-19-billion-chickens-4\">[4]</a>&nbsp;There are numerous&nbsp;<a href=\"https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Cultural_references_to_chickens\">cultural references to chickens</a>&nbsp;&ndash; in&nbsp;<a href=\"https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Myth\">myth</a>,&nbsp;<a href=\"https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Folklore\">folklore</a>&nbsp;and&nbsp;<a href=\"https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Religion\">religion</a>, and in&nbsp;<a href=\"https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Language\">language</a>&nbsp;and&nbsp;<a href=\"https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Literature\">literature</a>.</p>\r\n\r\n<p>Genetic studies have pointed to multiple maternal origins in South Asia, Southeast Asia, and East Asia,<a href=\"https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Chicken#cite_note-Xiang-5\">[5]</a>&nbsp;but the&nbsp;<a href=\"https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Clade\">clade</a>&nbsp;found in the Americas, Europe, the Middle East and Africa originated from the&nbsp;<a href=\"https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Indian_subcontinent\">Indian subcontinent</a>. From&nbsp;<a href=\"https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_India\">ancient India</a>, the chicken spread to&nbsp;<a href=\"https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lydia\">Lydia</a>&nbsp;in western&nbsp;<a href=\"https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Anatolia\">Asia Minor</a>, and to Greece by the 5th century BC.<a href=\"https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Chicken#cite_note-6\">[6]</a>&nbsp;Fowl have been known in&nbsp;<a href=\"https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Egypt\">Egypt</a>&nbsp;since the mid-15th century BC, with the &quot;bird that gives birth every day&quot; having come from the land between&nbsp;<a href=\"https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Syria\">Syria</a>&nbsp;and&nbsp;<a href=\"https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Shinar\">Shinar</a>,&nbsp;<a href=\"https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Babylonia\">Babylonia</a>, according to the&nbsp;<a href=\"https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Annals_of_Thutmose_III\">annals of Thutmose III</a>.<a href=\"https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Chicken#cite_note-7\">[7]</a><a href=\"https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Chicken#cite_note-8\">[8]</a><a href=\"https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Chicken#cite_note-RoehrigDreyfus2005-9\">[9]</a></p>',	1,	0,	'13,8,12,9,6,11',	1,	NULL,	'',	'{\"average\":4,\"total_reviews\":4}',	'1635491861.jpeg',	0,	NULL,	NULL),

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `product_connections`;
CREATE TABLE `product_connections` (
  `id` bigint(20) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `product_id` bigint(20) unsigned NOT NULL,
  `category_id` bigint(20) unsigned NOT NULL,
  `created_at` datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  `updated_at` datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `product_id` (`product_id`),
  KEY `category_id` (`category_id`),
  CONSTRAINT `product_connections_ibfk_3` FOREIGN KEY (`product_id`) REFERENCES `products` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE ON UPDATE CASCADE,
  CONSTRAINT `product_connections_ibfk_4` FOREIGN KEY (`category_id`) REFERENCES `categories` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE ON UPDATE CASCADE
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `recipes`;
CREATE TABLE `recipes` (
  `id` int(11) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `title` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `image` varchar(255) NOT NULL DEFAULT 'default.png',
  `gallery` varchar(255) NOT NULL DEFAULT 'default.png',
  `rating` int(11) NOT NULL DEFAULT '5',
  `position` int(11) NOT NULL DEFAULT '1',
  `time` varchar(100) DEFAULT NULL,
  `description` text,
  `status` tinyint(1) DEFAULT '1',
  `difficulty` varchar(30) DEFAULT 'EASY',
  `created_at` datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  `updated_at` datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `referrals`;
CREATE TABLE `referrals` (
  `id` bigint(20) unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `refer_from` bigint(20) unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `refer_to` bigint(20) unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `status` tinyint(4) NOT NULL DEFAULT '1',
  `created_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `updated_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `earn_points` double(8,2) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0.00',
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_unicode_ci;


DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `returns`;
CREATE TABLE `returns` (
  `id` bigint(20) unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `order_id` bigint(20) unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `order_history_id` bigint(20) unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `user_id` bigint(20) unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `product_id` bigint(20) unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `product_name` varchar(191) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `qty` int(11) NOT NULL DEFAULT '1',
  `unit` varchar(191) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `amount` double(16,2) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0.00',
  `product_image` varchar(191) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `issue` text COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci,
  `status` tinyint(4) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `is_refunded` tinyint(4) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `txn_id` bigint(20) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `created_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `updated_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_unicode_ci;


DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `reviews`;
CREATE TABLE `reviews` (
  `id` bigint(20) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `order_id` bigint(20) DEFAULT NULL,
  `product_id` bigint(20) unsigned NOT NULL,
  `user_id` bigint(20) unsigned NOT NULL,
  `rate` int(11) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `message` text COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL,
  `created_at` datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  `updated_at` datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `product_id` (`product_id`),
  KEY `user_id` (`user_id`),
  CONSTRAINT `reviews_ibfk_1` FOREIGN KEY (`product_id`) REFERENCES `products` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  CONSTRAINT `reviews_ibfk_2` FOREIGN KEY (`user_id`) REFERENCES `users` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_unicode_ci;


DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `review_to_users`;
CREATE TABLE `review_to_users` (
  `id` int(11) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `user_id` bigint(20) unsigned NOT NULL,
  `deliveryboy_id` int(11) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `order_id` bigint(20) unsigned NOT NULL,
  `rate` int(11) NOT NULL DEFAULT '1',
  `message` text COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci,
  `created_at` datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  `updated_at` datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `user_id` (`user_id`),
  KEY `order_id` (`order_id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_unicode_ci;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `settings`;
CREATE TABLE `settings` (
  `id` bigint(20) unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `app_name` varchar(191) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL,
  `logo` varchar(255) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `favicon` varchar(255) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `support_email` varchar(255) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `support_phone` varchar(255) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `terms` longtext COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci,
  `privacy_policy` longtext COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci,
  `shipping_policy` longtext COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci,
  `payment_policy` longtext COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci,
  `promise` longtext COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci,
  `delivery_policy` longtext COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci,
  `about_us` longtext COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci,
  `about_us_video` varchar(255) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT 'http://katlego.in/katlego_video.mp4',
  `invite_friends` longtext COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci,
  `referral_rewards` double(8,2) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0.00',
  `loyality_rewards` double(8,2) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0.00',
  `delivery_charges` double(16,2) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0.00',
  `splashing_text` text COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci,
  `cashback_signup` float(16,2) DEFAULT '0.00',
  `address` varchar(200) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `office_week` varchar(50) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `office_time` varchar(50) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `sunday_time` varchar(50) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_unicode_ci;

  `image` varchar(150) DEFAULT 'default.png',

  `status` tinyint(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT '1',
  `position` int(11) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `created_at` datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  `updated_at` datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1;

  `id` bigint(20) unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `user_id` bigint(20) unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `order_id` bigint(20) unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `order_txn_id` varchar(191) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `txn_name` varchar(191) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT '',
  `payment_mode` varchar(191) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT 'online' COMMENT 'online,cod,wallet',
  `type` varchar(191) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT 'credit' COMMENT 'credit,debit',
  `old_wallet` double(16,2) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0.00',
  `txn_amount` double(16,2) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0.00',
  `update_wallet` double(16,2) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0.00',
  `status` tinyint(4) NOT NULL DEFAULT '1' COMMENT '1->success,2->failed',
  `txn_mode` varchar(191) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT 'other' COMMENT 'credit_card,debit_card,ne_banking,UPI,other',
  `txn_for` varchar(191) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `bank_name` varchar(191) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `bank_txn_id` varchar(191) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `ifsc` varchar(191) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `account` varchar(191) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `created_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `updated_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `wallet_type` tinyint(1) DEFAULT '1' COMMENT '1->wallet,2->cashback_wallet',
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_unicode_ci;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `user_logins`;
CREATE TABLE `user_logins` (
  `id` bigint(20) unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `user_id` bigint(20) unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `device_id` varchar(191) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `device_type` varchar(191) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `device_token` varchar(191) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `model_name` varchar(191) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `ip_address` varchar(191) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `is_login` int(11) NOT NULL DEFAULT '1',
  `created_at` datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  `updated_at` datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_unicode_ci;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `vacations`;
CREATE TABLE `vacations` (
  `id` bigint(20) unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `user_id` bigint(20) unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `start_date` datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  `end_date` datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  `other_data` text COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci,
  `created_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `updated_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_unicode_ci;


DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `wishlists`;
CREATE TABLE `wishlists` (
  `id` bigint(20) unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `user_id` bigint(20) unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `product_id` bigint(20) unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `status` tinyint(4) NOT NULL DEFAULT '1',
  `created_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `updated_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `wishlists_user_id_foreign` (`user_id`),
  KEY `wishlists_product_id_foreign` (`product_id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_unicode_ci;
